        <script>
            $(document).ready(function() {
                $('div.cpm-text-description p').each(function () {
                    replaceConsentHtmlContent(this);
                });

                $('span.text-truncate-container p').each(function () {
                    replaceConsentHtmlContent(this);
                });

                $('#textLegalContent .consentText p').each(function() {
                    replaceConsentHtmlContent(this);
                });

                $('#agreement.legalText p').each(function() {
                    replaceConsentHtmlContent(this);
                });
            });

            function replaceConsentHtmlContent(thisObj) {
                let htmlContent = {};
                $(thisObj).children().each(function (index) {
                    let param = "anchor"+index
                    $(this).html(parseHtmlContent($(this).html()))
                    htmlContent[param] = $(this)
                    $(this).replaceWith( param);
                })
                let inputContent = $(thisObj).html();
                let textContent = parseHtmlContent(inputContent);


                $(thisObj).html(textContent);
                inputContent = $(thisObj).html();
                $.each(htmlContent, function (key, data) {
                    inputContent =inputContent.replace(key , data[0].outerHTML);
                });
                $(thisObj).html(inputContent);
            }

            function parseHtmlContent(input) {
                let doc = new DOMParser().parseFromString(input, "text/html");
                return doc.documentElement.textContent;
            }
        </script>

        function getCookiePref(cookieName) {
          let cookie = {};
          document.cookie.split(';').forEach(function(el) {
            let [key,value] = el.split('=');
            cookie[key.trim()] = value;
          })
          return cookie[cookieName];
        }

    <script>
        window.addEventListener("load", function() {
            let isConsentProvided = false;
            if(typeof truste !== "undefined"){
                const TRUST_FUNCTIONAL = 2;
                let result = truste.cma.callApi("getConsentDecision", window.location.host);
                if (result.consentDecision >= TRUST_FUNCTIONAL) {
                    isConsentProvided = true;
                    if(window.location.href.includes('#')){
                        var scrollDivId= window.location.href.split("#")[1];
                        $('html, body').animate({
                            scrollTop: $("#"+scrollDivId).offset().top
                        }, 2000);
                    }
                }
            }
            if (document.referrer && !document.referrer.includes(".hays.")) {
                localStorage.setItem("hays-referrer-ext", document.referrer);
            }
            if (!isConsentProvided) {
                window['ac_client_disable_tracking'] = true;
            }
        });

        //handling the Trust Arc...
        window.addEventListener("message", function(event){
            let eventDataJson  = null;
            try {
                eventDataJson = JSON.parse(event.data);
            } catch(exp) {

            }

            if (eventDataJson && eventDataJson.source === 'preference_manager'
                && eventDataJson.message === 'submit_preferences') {
                window.location.reload();
            }


        });
    </script>

<script>

    var parentHeight = 0;
    $(".nav-list__item").mouseenter(function () {
        if($(this).hasClass('nav-list__item_child')) {
            var lengthOfChild =  $(this).children().length;
            if (lengthOfChild > 1) {
                var childHeight =  $(this).children('div.container-grid-third').children('ul.nav-list__third').height();
                childHeight =  1.1 * childHeight;
                if(parentHeight == 0) {
                    parentHeight = $(this).parents('ul.nav-list__first').parent('.container-grid-first').height();
                }
                var height = Math.max(childHeight, parentHeight);
                $(this).parents('ul.nav-list__first').parent('.container-grid-first').height(height);
            }else {
                if (parentHeight != 0) {
                    $(this).parents('ul.nav-list__first').parent('.container-grid-first').height(parentHeight);
                    parentHeight = 0;
                }

            }
        }

    })


    $("#accessibility").click(function () {
        $("#eyeAble_columID").css("display", "block");
    });

</script>

    <!-- suchbar {{{ -->

            <script type="text/javascript">
                // Generate the searchHistory module
                $(function () {
                    $('#searchbarForm').searchHistory({
                        'sendWhenSelect': true,
                        'maxShowNum': 5,
                        'actionByCall': true,
                        'lang': "en_GB"
                    });

                    $("#what").click(function (e) {
                        if ($("#what").val().length > 0) {
                            $('#searchbarForm').searchHistory('close');
                        } else {
                            $('#searchbarForm').searchHistory('open');
                        }
                    });

                    $("#what").keyup(function (e) {
                        if ($("#what").val().length > 0) {
                            $('#searchbarForm').searchHistory('close');
                        } else {
                            $('#searchbarForm').searchHistory('open');
                        }
                    });

                });

            </script>

</ul>
	
</nav>

	
	
					
				
			
		
	
	


	</div>

			</div>
		
	</div>
</section>
	

		
		







	</div>






                    </div>

<p><strong>Technical writer (m/f/d)</strong></p></h1>

They often work in the technical documentation departments of large industrial companies. The main task of technical writers is to explain the functions of complex devices in understandable language and make them accessible to users. This enables them to use the product without any problems.</div></div><style>.component-paragraph img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-ae8c0525-c359-b891-0d52-07266ce3e9ca " style=""><div id="fragment-ac5d363b-d5a6-f383-e2b0-ee6e704b42dc"> <div class="py-2"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-75a2bee2-3b15-3205-baf9-0c6538776632 lfr-layout-structure-item-container " style=""><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-html lfr-layout-structure-item-5424b1d2-5424-2bf5-4201-8716b86adf24 " style=""><div id="fragment-27563f8d-e059-42cc-2dd3-afd3e123f17f"> <div class="component-html" data-lfr-editable-id="element-html" data-lfr-editable-type="html">

            setTimeout(function(){ $('.c-success-story_active-story').click() }, 400);
        }
    });

    $('.c-success-story_active-story').click(function() {
        if ($('.c-success-story_active-story-icon').hasClass('glyphicon-chevron-up')){
             $('.c-success-story_active-story-icon').removeClass('glyphicon-chevron-up');
             $('.c-success-story_active-story-icon').addClass('glyphicon-chevron-down');
             $(this).css('background-color', '#EFEFEF');
             $('.c-success-story_active-story-title').show()
             $('.c-success-story_active-story-description').show()
             $('.c-success-story_active-story-icon').css('color','#009FDA')
        }else{
            $('.c-success-story_active-story-icon').addClass('glyphicon-chevron-up');
            $('.c-success-story_active-story-icon').removeClass('glyphicon-chevron-down');
            $(this).css('background-color', 'transparent')
            $('.c-success-story_active-story-title').hide()
            $('.c-success-story_active-story-description').hide()
            $('.c-success-story_active-story-icon').css('color','#FFFFFF')
        }
        $( ".c-success-story__tabs" ).animate({
            height: "toggle"
        }, 400, function() {
        });
    });

    $stories.each(function(index, element) {
        var $story = $(element),
            $masters = $story.find('[data-tab-master]'),
            $allSlaves = $story.find('[data-tab-slave]'),
            $headlines = $story.find('.c-success-story__tab-headline'),
            height = 0;

        $headlines.each(function(i) {
            headlineHeight = $headlines.eq(i).height();
            height = (headlineHeight > height) ? headlineHeight : height;
        });

        $masters.each(function(i, el) {

            /* tabnav functionality */
            (function(index, $master) {
                var slaveIndex = $master.attr("data-tab-master"),
                    $slaves = $story.find('[data-tab-slave="' + slaveIndex + '"]');

                if (i === 0) {
                    $master.addClass('-active');
                    $slaves.addClass('-active');
                    $('.c-success-story_active-story-title').text($master.children().children("div.c-success-story__tab-author-name").text().trim());
                    var authorPostion = $master.children().children("div.c-success-story__tab-author-position").text().trim()
                    if(authorPostion !="" && authorPostion !=null){
                        $('.c-success-story_active-story-description').append("<br/>"+authorPostion)
                    }

                };

                $master.off('click.SUCCESSSTORY');
                $master.on('click.SUCCESSSTORY', function(event) {
                    if ($master.hasClass('active')) return;
                    $masters.removeClass('-active');
                    $allSlaves.removeClass('-active');
                    $master.addClass('-active');
                    $('.c-success-story_active-story-title').text($master.children().children("div.c-success-story__tab-author-name").text().trim())
                    $('.c-success-story_active-story-description').text('')
                    var authorPostion = $master.children().children("div.c-success-story__tab-author-position").text().trim()
                    if(authorPostion !="" && authorPostion !=null){
                        $('.c-success-story_active-story-description').append("<br/>"+authorPostion)
                    }
                    $slaves.addClass('-active');
                });
            })(i, $(el))
        });

        /* same height */
        $(window).resize(function() {
            $headlines.removeAttr('height');
            $headlines.each(function(i) {
                headlineHeight = $headlines.eq(i).height();
                height = (headlineHeight > height) ? headlineHeight : height;
            });
            $headlines.height(height);
        });

        $headlines.height(height);
    });

<h2>
 What is a technical writer?  <br /><strong>Definition and overview </strong>
</h2></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-528e9a82-07d2-c421-a195-29fc017f45c3 " style=""><div id="fragment-349a25ad-4eec-153f-ec91-6261edd843e4"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text"><p paraeid="{afea1427-6066-4c03-b194-12191f6a6320}{155}" paraid="474751995">A technical writer writes <strong>comprehensible instructions for technical products, </strong>often called information products, to make them easier for users to use. These can be <strong>operating, assembly and design instructions, as well as safety regulations and training material.&nbsp;</strong></p>

<p paraeid="{afea1427-6066-4c03-b194-12191f6a6320}{173}" paraid="806161448">The aim is to explain technically complex products such as smartphones, cars, kitchen appliances or medical technology as clearly as possible for the respective target group. In addition to traditional operating instructions, they can also create graphics, videos, apps or even augmented reality.&nbsp;</p>

<p paraeid="{afea1427-6066-4c03-b194-12191f6a6320}{199}" paraid="189736706">Technical writers must have <strong>a very good technical understanding </strong>of their product. After all, they have the task of <strong>presenting and explaining</strong> complex issues and procedures as <strong>clearly as possible.</strong> In addition, they must be able to conduct in-depth research and work well with content management systems (CMS). Their well thought-out concepts simplify the everyday lives of countless customers, who are ultimately able to deal with complicated technology more quickly and easily.&nbsp;</p>
</div></div><style>.component-paragraph img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div></div> 
 </div>
</div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-396cb1a7-8867-86a7-6de4-94f40ee62f61 " style=""><div id="fragment-a55b889e-ef6b-7e72-870f-b460a2b34fc4"> <div class="py-2"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-fd2d9f12-9115-1add-cdf7-2e180f58ff64 " style=""><div id="fragment-754eb89f-7ff8-a6c6-874d-ad3974b8b9d5"> <div class="py-2"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-e9147f8b-5d8d-f358-aaa9-cc634d866405 lfr-layout-structure-item-container " style=""><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-h-dropzone-990px lfr-layout-structure-item-d91ea917-bed8-1745-8149-8efcdd3f96e9 " style=""><div id="fragment-594c1be2-bc32-1204-f397-140b57dbf931"> <div class="fragment_1">  <div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-html lfr-layout-structure-item-8fb86e0e-8005-fa80-c5f6-1d4e4e0cd5b8 " style=""><div id="fragment-34e156b7-fd74-0f54-4cbf-ff12d6488b42"> <div class="component-html" data-lfr-editable-id="element-html" data-lfr-editable-type="html"><span id="gehalt"></span></div></div><style>.component-html img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-html lfr-layout-structure-item-1c980391-51b0-45a5-ca26-840578df8102 " style=""><div id="fragment-cf08fa9c-93a6-df55-55a2-bda73b2c3e85"> <div class="component-html" data-lfr-editable-id="element-html" data-lfr-editable-type="html">




<h2>
<strong>Technical writer salary:  </strong><br />What you can earn </h2></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-d403f583-41e2-ccdb-02dd-9b20b29529eb " style=""><div id="fragment-538d2e19-51df-2bdd-510f-9c48feb13879"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text"><p paraeid="{ec1edebe-309b-4ab9-9070-eeff90cdbf11}{2}" paraid="1984459063">The salary of technical writers in Germany is around <strong>€46,800 gross per year.&nbsp;</strong></p>

<p paraeid="{ec1edebe-309b-4ab9-9070-eeff90cdbf11}{18}" paraid="1412191276">However, the salary prospects for technical writers vary greatly. In smaller companies, the average gross salary is around €38,000 per year. Employees in larger companies can achieve an annual salary of around €58,000, depending on their professional experience.&nbsp;</p>

<p paraeid="{ec1edebe-309b-4ab9-9070-eeff90cdbf11}{34}" paraid="1134955597">In addition, the salary depends on the training, the industry and the location of the company. Experienced technical writers with specialised skills or knowledge in a sought-after industry can often negotiate a higher salary.&nbsp;</p>
</div></div><style>.component-paragraph img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-e0967654-cab4-3a5e-de1f-4c8712af5e5d " style=""><div id="fragment-422fb13e-b63f-c1fd-b650-f416ea61d233"> <div class="py-2"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-fafdb4f3-3df7-5319-0cb2-6788008a278a lfr-layout-structure-item-row " style=""><div class="row align-items-lg-start align-items-sm-start align-items-start align-items-md-start flex-lg-row flex-sm-row flex-row flex-md-row"><div class="col col-lg-2 col-sm-12 col-12 col-md-2"><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-b59b3ded-4fa1-1110-a7e3-8f8768f75210 lfr-layout-structure-item-container " style=""><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-e9c7d4ea-6282-67cf-c636-4201b9d53704 " style=""><div id="fragment-4805e393-3946-5368-08e4-9de0387c0630"> <div class="py-1"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-image lfr-layout-structure-item-67a19cd2-2578-bd86-aa61-840926aa41d2 " style=""><div id="fragment-f683b7a5-45ba-b23e-7eb9-32c4de628fd5"> <div class="component-image overflow-hidden">

<h3>
Starting salary as a technical writer: Junior technical writer salary
</h3></div></div><style>.component-html img {
	max-width: 100%;

<h2>
  What does a technical writer do? <br /><strong>Tasks and daily routine</strong> 
</h2></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-95b0b48b-a95b-87b0-6f83-c67a78dc6f16 " style=""><div id="fragment-5211aa21-b384-2736-ca4d-8398a14d25bc"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text"><p paraeid="{ec1edebe-309b-4ab9-9070-eeff90cdbf11}{112}" paraid="1212684709">Technical writers act as generalists who take care of the <strong>entire technical documentation process</strong>. This means that they design, create and update technical documentation such as operating instructions, installation and assembly instructions or training documents. This is because information products such as software or complex machines are not self-explanatory.&nbsp;</p>

<p paraeid="{ec1edebe-309b-4ab9-9070-eeff90cdbf11}{128}" paraid="286044538">In order to achieve this, technical writers have to develop concepts and research product information, as well as being in constant dialogue with developers. For many technical writers, <strong>scientific journalism</strong> is also part of their everyday work. They mainly write guides or articles for specialist journals.&nbsp;</p>
</div></div><style>.component-paragraph img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-54139010-9205-0520-509e-59d7f0ad70fe " style=""><div id="fragment-1ddc80c1-e33a-37a9-1115-70f827a51e28"> <div class="py-1"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-d1dbb532-28f6-8863-9420-cc7a24680523 lfr-layout-structure-item-row " style=""><div class="row align-items-lg-start align-items-sm-start align-items-start align-items-md-start flex-lg-row flex-sm-row flex-row flex-md-row"><div class="col col-lg-9 col-sm-12 col-12 col-md-9"><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-021b02c2-23cc-e36a-7b57-d70fd7fe2328 " style=""><div id="fragment-4c85c82c-3c32-6df7-1f30-ef4f6ad0fe0e"> <div class="py-1"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-4a688ba4-b05c-cab2-0db3-bfdcceaa6dba " style=""><div id="fragment-8212fc1c-9abc-a323-0021-d3ebf5388c43"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text">The most important <strong>tasks of technical writers</strong> on the job are:&nbsp;</div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-1187021f-187b-0330-406e-81cffd410c8d " style=""><div id="fragment-8c8c704a-ea80-a197-a40b-dce62100e55e"> <div class="py-1"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-4e2c1526-4235-b8f2-02c9-980101e39a71 " style=""><div id="fragment-aaf5cdd9-36f2-6b09-60bf-1d51ad76ffe0"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text"><ul>
	<li aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-level="1" data-aria-posinset="1" data-font="Symbol" data-leveltext="" data-list-defn-props="{&quot;335552541&quot;:1,&quot;335559685&quot;:720,&quot;335559991&quot;:360,&quot;469769226&quot;:&quot;Symbol&quot;,&quot;469769242&quot;:[8226],&quot;469777803&quot;:&quot;left&quot;,&quot;469777804&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;469777815&quot;:&quot;multilevel&quot;}" data-listid="1" role="listitem">
	<p paraeid="{ec1edebe-309b-4ab9-9070-eeff90cdbf11}{162}" paraid="1585493304">Research work&nbsp;</p>
	</li>
	<li aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-level="1" data-aria-posinset="8" data-font="Symbol" data-leveltext="" data-list-defn-props="{&quot;335552541&quot;:1,&quot;335559685&quot;:720,&quot;335559991&quot;:360,&quot;469769226&quot;:&quot;Symbol&quot;,&quot;469769242&quot;:[8226],&quot;469777803&quot;:&quot;left&quot;,&quot;469777804&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;469777815&quot;:&quot;multilevel&quot;}" data-listid="1" role="listitem">
	<p paraeid="{ec1edebe-309b-4ab9-9070-eeff90cdbf11}{211}" paraid="599008635">Translations of already created content&nbsp;</p>
	</li>
	<li aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-level="1" data-aria-posinset="7" data-font="Symbol" data-leveltext="" data-list-defn-props="{&quot;335552541&quot;:1,&quot;335559685&quot;:720,&quot;335559991&quot;:360,&quot;469769226&quot;:&quot;Symbol&quot;,&quot;469769242&quot;:[8226],&quot;469777803&quot;:&quot;left&quot;,&quot;469777804&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;469777815&quot;:&quot;multilevel&quot;}" data-listid="1" role="listitem">
	<p paraeid="{ec1edebe-309b-4ab9-9070-eeff90cdbf11}{205}" paraid="1158269633">Exchange with developers&nbsp;</p>
	</li>
	<li aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-level="1" data-aria-posinset="6" data-font="Symbol" data-leveltext="" data-list-defn-props="{&quot;335552541&quot;:1,&quot;335559685&quot;:720,&quot;335559991&quot;:360,&quot;469769226&quot;:&quot;Symbol&quot;,&quot;469769242&quot;:[8226],&quot;469777803&quot;:&quot;left&quot;,&quot;469777804&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;469777815&quot;:&quot;multilevel&quot;}" data-listid="1" role="listitem">
	<p paraeid="{ec1edebe-309b-4ab9-9070-eeff90cdbf11}{199}" paraid="388634853">Compliance with legal regulations&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
	</li>
	<li aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-level="1" data-aria-posinset="5" data-font="Symbol" data-leveltext="" data-list-defn-props="{&quot;335552541&quot;:1,&quot;335559685&quot;:720,&quot;335559991&quot;:360,&quot;469769226&quot;:&quot;Symbol&quot;,&quot;469769242&quot;:[8226],&quot;469777803&quot;:&quot;left&quot;,&quot;469777804&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;469777815&quot;:&quot;multilevel&quot;}" data-listid="1" role="listitem">
	<p paraeid="{ec1edebe-309b-4ab9-9070-eeff90cdbf11}{193}" paraid="1954616753">Creation of multimedia content&nbsp;</p>
	</li>
	<li aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-level="1" data-aria-posinset="4" data-font="Symbol" data-leveltext="" data-list-defn-props="{&quot;335552541&quot;:1,&quot;335559685&quot;:720,&quot;335559991&quot;:360,&quot;469769226&quot;:&quot;Symbol&quot;,&quot;469769242&quot;:[8226],&quot;469777803&quot;:&quot;left&quot;,&quot;469777804&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;469777815&quot;:&quot;multilevel&quot;}" data-listid="1" role="listitem">
	<p paraeid="{ec1edebe-309b-4ab9-9070-eeff90cdbf11}{182}" paraid="1078814543">Creation of writerial content&nbsp;</p>
	</li>
	<li aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-level="1" data-aria-posinset="3" data-font="Symbol" data-leveltext="" data-list-defn-props="{&quot;335552541&quot;:1,&quot;335559685&quot;:720,&quot;335559991&quot;:360,&quot;469769226&quot;:&quot;Symbol&quot;,&quot;469769242&quot;:[8226],&quot;469777803&quot;:&quot;left&quot;,&quot;469777804&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;469777815&quot;:&quot;multilevel&quot;}" data-listid="1" role="listitem">
	<p paraeid="{ec1edebe-309b-4ab9-9070-eeff90cdbf11}{176}" paraid="1635002568">Creation of technical documentation&nbsp;</p>
	</li>
	<li aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-level="1" data-aria-posinset="2" data-font="Symbol" data-leveltext="" data-list-defn-props="{&quot;335552541&quot;:1,&quot;335559685&quot;:720,&quot;335559991&quot;:360,&quot;469769226&quot;:&quot;Symbol&quot;,&quot;469769242&quot;:[8226],&quot;469777803&quot;:&quot;left&quot;,&quot;469777804&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;469777815&quot;:&quot;multilevel&quot;}" data-listid="1" role="listitem">
	<p paraeid="{ec1edebe-309b-4ab9-9070-eeff90cdbf11}{170}" paraid="179642120">Development of concepts&nbsp;</p>
	</li>
</ul>
</div></div></div></div><div class="col col-lg-3 col-sm-12 col-12 col-md-3"><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-4fa50d4d-9a74-a982-9163-43e8ed178f5c " style=""><div id="fragment-ea332688-d748-561f-512b-dbaa7304cbd5"> <div class="py-1"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-65d0efbf-1817-4078-2329-64a6409f0076 " style=""><div id="fragment-afef8457-a11d-87c9-7f0b-df5b3c3d6a6a"> <div class="py-3"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-image lfr-layout-structure-item-0d12514f-d21c-a1d3-08b6-147dd5197a6d " style=""><div id="fragment-72ac9279-eca2-8772-ac9f-9a15dda01a79"> <div class="component-image overflow-hidden">
	<picture data-fileentryid="3448402684"><source media="(max-width:300px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3448402684/thumbnail-300x300/pfeil-dreiblaue-dreiecke-365x197.png?t=1691131430984" /><source media="(max-width:365px) and (min-width:300px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3448402684/1000px-till-1280px-width/pfeil-dreiblaue-dreiecke-365x197.png?t=1691131430984" /><source media="(max-width:365px) and (min-width:365px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3448402684/480px-width/pfeil-dreiblaue-dreiecke-365x197.png?t=1691131430984" /><source media="(max-width:365px) and (min-width:365px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3448402684/980px-width/pfeil-dreiblaue-dreiecke-365x197.png?t=1691131430984" /><source media="(max-width:365px) and (min-width:365px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3448402684/high-resolution/pfeil-dreiblaue-dreiecke-365x197.png?t=1691131430984" /><source media="(max-width:365px) and (min-width:365px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3448402684/Preview-1000x0/pfeil-dreiblaue-dreiecke-365x197.png?t=1691131430984" /><img alt="" class="w-100" data-lfr-editable-id="image-square" data-lfr-editable-type="image" src="/documents/d/global/pfeil-dreiblaue-dreiecke-365x197?imagePreview=1" loading="lazy" /></picture>

	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-4ccedf97-6e53-e3bf-3465-8678f1be76bc lfr-layout-structure-item-container " style=""><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-html lfr-layout-structure-item-00310751-29b4-1e18-17a8-84ac67171b3c " style=""><div id="fragment-d0e081d3-5375-37fa-f364-cee0344883e7"> <div class="component-html" data-lfr-editable-id="element-html" data-lfr-editable-type="html">




<h2>
<strong>How do you become a technical writer? </strong><br /> Training, studies &amp; further education
</h2>
</div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-faab2d94-b3e3-196e-538d-93c4f2a2332f " style=""><div id="fragment-b176c481-054f-cea6-055f-2f9ac6fc7b7a"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text"><p paraeid="{ec1edebe-309b-4ab9-9070-eeff90cdbf11}{237}" paraid="1077958073">In Germany, the demand for qualified technical writers is currently high. In addition to <strong>graduates of degree programmes such as Technical Communication, career changers are also</strong> in demand. Additional training and formal qualifications in technical communication are important for lateral entry.&nbsp;</p>

<p paraeid="{ec1edebe-309b-4ab9-9070-eeff90cdbf11}{251}" paraid="2133164539">Many companies have particularly good opportunities for female engineers and specialists with technical vocational training. Software companies are also increasingly looking for employees with a non-technical background.&nbsp;</p>

<p paraeid="{8e1b0446-9ca6-4065-b049-98cf64a47c8d}{8}" paraid="1090942454">In order to be successful in the job in the long term, it is also advisable to network with other people and to continuously develop your skills. Due to innovations and further developments in technology, technical writers need to keep their knowledge up to date. For easy networking, <a href="https://www.tekom.de/die-tekom/werde-teil-der-community/mitglied-werden" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">tekom</a> offers various memberships - even free of charge for students and trainees.&nbsp;</p>
</div></div><style>.component-paragraph img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-19bb585a-7754-d176-bcca-a28e25bc7ea3 " style=""><div id="fragment-14cac4ab-2167-4d4d-f661-ecd91ac8c41a"> <div class="py-2"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-html lfr-layout-structure-item-99147d33-4f03-fd41-b24f-afe0c82bf62e " style=""><div id="fragment-dcce91d1-499b-af7e-157e-6ce7a774242f"> <div class="component-html" data-lfr-editable-id="element-html" data-lfr-editable-type="html">




<h3>
Further training to become a technical writer: the practical route </h3>
</div></div><style>.component-html img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-3dfdc23f-82ef-3623-6789-2598e3ffa14d lfr-layout-structure-item-row " style=""><div class="row align-items-lg-start align-items-sm-start align-items-start align-items-md-start flex-lg-row flex-sm-row flex-row flex-md-row"><div class="col col-lg-8 col-sm-12 col-12 col-md-8"><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-7d5c588a-d5b9-29b6-7781-6ef41c007465 " style=""><div id="fragment-f7c7cf8c-f596-69df-28a3-8fa008654d28"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text"><p paraeid="{8e1b0446-9ca6-4065-b049-98cf64a47c8d}{41}" paraid="448123063">In addition to a degree programme, <strong>further training to become a technical writer</strong> is also a good way<strong> to start your career.</strong> Institutes offer training to become a technical writer both <strong>full-time and part-time</strong>. The main advantage of this type of training is the targeted learning of all the important skills for the job and the opportunity to gain practical experience at the same time.&nbsp;</p>

<p paraeid="{8e1b0446-9ca6-4065-b049-98cf64a47c8d}{61}" paraid="1276426789">For a lateral entry as a technical writer, a full-time training programme lasting several months is suitable, while for people with professional experience but without a degree, a part-time training programme might be more suitable.&nbsp;</p>

<p paraeid="{8e1b0446-9ca6-4065-b049-98cf64a47c8d}{79}" paraid="2116933213">At the end of the training programme, we recommend taking the <strong>certification exam organised by tekom e.V.,</strong> for which you register independently. The certificate is internationally recognised and proves relevant knowledge in technical writerial offices.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
</div></div><style>.component-paragraph img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div></div><div class="col col-lg-4 col-sm-12 col-12 col-md-4"><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-b6750c3f-6e29-3d4a-35af-d5c694256cdf " style=""><div id="fragment-1636dca2-ce30-cae6-b2c0-055b89438433"> <div class="py-1"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-image lfr-layout-structure-item-4c44301f-558e-7473-8406-9c2def2db23c " style=""><div id="fragment-9c41b7cf-75cd-6cb6-9261-a997d7e19b14"> <div class="component-image overflow-hidden">
	<picture data-fileentryid="3465121703"><source media="(max-width:300px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3465121703/thumbnail-300x300/Isometric+Illustration_Neurodiversity.png?t=1722841362527" /><source media="(max-width:480px) and (min-width:300px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3465121703/480px-width/Isometric+Illustration_Neurodiversity.png?t=1722841362527" /><source media="(max-width:500px) and (min-width:480px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3465121703/1000px-till-1280px-width/Isometric+Illustration_Neurodiversity.png?t=1722841362527" /><source media="(max-width:500px) and (min-width:500px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3465121703/980px-width/Isometric+Illustration_Neurodiversity.png?t=1722841362527" /><source media="(max-width:500px) and (min-width:500px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3465121703/high-resolution/Isometric+Illustration_Neurodiversity.png?t=1722841362527" /><source media="(max-width:500px) and (min-width:500px)" srcset="/o/adaptive-media/image/3465121703/Preview-1000x0/Isometric+Illustration_Neurodiversity.png?t=1722841362527" /><img alt="" class="w-100" data-lfr-editable-id="image-square" data-lfr-editable-type="image" src="/documents/d/global/isometric-illustration_neurodiversity-png?imagePreview=1" loading="lazy" /></picture>
</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-spacer lfr-layout-structure-item-7ca6af0f-4f1c-ed17-2333-542df5860bde " style=""><div id="fragment-95094420-801c-287a-2b84-0e1d6872d2cc"> <div class="py-2"></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-html lfr-layout-structure-item-b4fef206-b6ef-0afa-23d0-a366820aa313 " style=""><div id="fragment-ba906ddd-2372-b3f7-8626-0b69de0095e9"> <div class="component-html" data-lfr-editable-id="element-html" data-lfr-editable-type="html">




<h3>
  Studium: Technischer Redakteur auf akademischen Weg werden
</h3>
</div></div><style>.component-html img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-3c1f1865-e0a1-3572-e815-1fb4e96f7821 lfr-layout-structure-item-row " style=""><div class="row align-items-lg-start align-items-sm-start align-items-start align-items-md-start flex-lg-row flex-sm-row flex-row flex-md-row"><div class="col col-lg-8 col-sm-12 col-12 col-md-8"><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-216ec9a4-8127-ad4c-e4cc-6424a47ede3c " style=""><div id="fragment-2bc7f955-5883-113e-084c-e4eb818d1342"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text"><p paraeid="{8e1b0446-9ca6-4065-b049-98cf64a47c8d}{127}" paraid="1914592301">If you want to become a technical writer via the academic route, you are well advised to study technical communication or technical editing. Engineering degree programmes are also suitable for pursuing this career path. Generally speaking, a degree programme is very popular with technical writers in HR departments.&nbsp;</p>

<p paraeid="{8e1b0446-9ca6-4065-b049-98cf64a47c8d}{143}" paraid="297997580">Suitable <strong>degree programmes for prospective technical writers:&nbsp;</strong></p>
</div></div><style>.component-paragraph img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-23506952-b0b1-5766-3505-cad32206d287 " style=""><div id="fragment-941bcfd1-42f6-2d4b-2575-13e70b82eb81"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text"><ul>
	<li style="display: block; width: 0px; height: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; margin: 0px; position: absolute; top: 0px; left: -9999px; opacity: 0; overflow: hidden;">&nbsp;</li>
	<li paraeid="{8e1b0446-9ca6-4065-b049-98cf64a47c8d}{159}" paraid="1035818998"><a href="https://f1.hs-hannover.de/en/course/degree-courses-and-programmes/bachelors-degree-courses/technical-information-design-and-technical-communication-itr" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Technical Information Design and Technical Editing (ITR) at Hanover University of Applied Sciences and Arts</a> (Bachelor)&nbsp;</li>
	<li paraeid="{8e1b0446-9ca6-4065-b049-98cf64a47c8d}{168}" paraid="602164778"><a href="https://www.h-brs.de/en/iwk/study/bachelor/technical-journalism" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Technical Journalism at Bonn-Rhein-Sieg University of Applied Sciences</a> (Bachelor)&nbsp;</li>
	<li paraeid="{8e1b0446-9ca6-4065-b049-98cf64a47c8d}{177}" paraid="144135146"><a href="https://mtik.rwth-aachen.de/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Human-Technology Interaction &amp; Communication at RWTH Aachen University</a> (Bachelor and/or Master)&nbsp;</li>
</ul>

<script type="text/javascript">
function submitForm() {
    $('.newsForm').addClass('submitted');
    AUI().use('aui-io-request', function(A) {
       const fetchMe = 'https://www.hays.de/en/job-profiles/technical-writer?p_p_id=de_hays_osgi_liferay_webform_newsletter_portlet_NewsLetterPortlet_INSTANCE_ptol&p_p_lifecycle=2&p_p_state=normal&p_p_mode=view&p_p_resource_id=saveData&p_p_cacheability=cacheLevelPage';
       $('.newsForm button[type=submit]').prop('disabled', true);
       

       $.ajax(fetchMe, {
            method: 'post',
            data: $("#_de_hays_osgi_liferay_webform_newsletter_portlet_NewsLetterPortlet_INSTANCE_ptol_fm").serialize(),
            beforeSend: function() {
                $('#message-div').empty();
            },
           success: function(data) {
                let content= JSON.parse(data);
                let wasSuccessful = content.successful;
                let text = content.message;
                let url = content.redirect;
                let messageDiv = $('#message-div');
                
                let successMessage, errorMessage;
                // enable button again
                $('.newsForm button[type=submit]').prop('disabled', false);
                $('.newsForm').removeClass('submitted');
        
                if(wasSuccessful) {
                    if(popUp === 'true'){
                        successMessage = $('<div id="confirmation" class="portlet-msg-success">' + text + '</div>');
                        messageDiv.append(successMessage);
                        $("#topformBody, #bottomformBody, #textLegalContent, .show-more").hide();
                    } else {
                        window.location.href=url;
                    }
                } else {
                    errorMessage = $('<div id="confirmation" class="portlet-msg-error">' + text + '</div>');
                    messageDiv.append(errorMessage);
                }
                
                /*if( /Android|webOS|iPhone|iPad|iPod|BlackBerry|IEMobile|Opera Mini/i.test(navigator.userAgent) ) {
                    document.getElementById("confirmation").scrollIntoView();
                }*/
           },
           error: function() {
            errorMessage = $('<div id="confirmation" class="portlet-msg-error">' + text + '</div>');
            messageDiv.append(errorMessage);
           }                        
        });
    });
}

    /*$(document).ready(function(){
        var errorMessage = 'This field is required.';
        var errorMessageRadio = 'error-field-anliegen';

        $("#submitButton").click(function(e) {
            var isReiterAktivSelect = false;
            var isRequired = false;
            var isAnrede = false;

            $(".padding-block .required-field").each(function() {
                if($(this).val() == "") {
                    isRequired = true;
                    $(this).parent().parent().find('.contact-input-label').addClass('contact-input-error-label-focus');
                    $(this).addClass('error-field');
                    $(this).parent().append('<div class="form-validator-stack help-block"><div role="alert" class="required">'+errorMessage+'</div></div>');
                }
            });

            if (isReiterAktivSelect) {
                $('html, body').animate({
                    scrollTop: $(".ReiterAktivSelect").offset().top - 50
                }, 1000);
            } else if (isAnrede) {
                $('html, body').animate({
                scrollTop: $(".anrede-flex-for-inputs").offset().top - 50
                }, 1000);
            } else if (isRequired) {
                $('html, body').animate({
                scrollTop: $(".padding-block .required-field").offset().top - 50
                }, 1000);
            }
            
            if (isReiterAktivSelect || isAnrede || isRequired) {
                e.preventDefault();
                e.stopPropagation();
                e.stopImmediatePropagation();
                return false;
            }
        });
    });*/

</script>

<script>

    let popUp = '';
    const htmlBody=document.querySelector("html");
    const htmlBodysc=document.querySelector("body");
    const bodyHeight= $(document).height();
    const popUpClose = function(){
        const popUpC = document.querySelector(".mainRow");
        popUpC.remove();
    }
    const mainDiv = document.querySelector(".newsletter-form");
    const form = document.querySelector(".newsForm");
    const myDiv = document.querySelector(".mainRow");
    const $openMe = $('#textLegalContent'),
        $submitButton = $('#submitButton'),
        openMeInitialHeight = $openMe.height();

    $('.show-more').on('click', function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        const $this = $(this);
        $this.closest('.ui-dialog').off('scroll').on('scroll', moveSubmitButton);

        $openMe.toggleClass('open');
        $this.toggleClass('open');
        if ($openMe.hasClass('open')) {
            $this.text($this.data('text-open'));
        } else {
            $this.text($this.data('text'));
        }
        moveSubmitButton();
    })

    $('.newsletter-portlet').on('dialogopen', function(){
        htmlBody.classList.add('hidescrl');
        htmlBodysc.classList.add('hidescrl');
        $('.ui-dialog').addClass('ui-dialog-popup');
        $('.body-shadow').addClass('box-body-shadow');
        $('.body-shadow').css('height', bodyHeight+600);
        $(document).scrollTop($('#newsletter-portlet').offset().top);
    });

    const moveSubmitButton = function() {
        $('#submitButton').css({bottom: '-'+$('.ui-dialog')[0].scrollTop + 'px'})
    }

    /*$('#btn-newsletterPopup-mobile').click(function(){
        htmlBody.classList.add('hidescrl');
        htmlBodysc.classList.add('hidescrl');
        $('.ui-dialog').addClass('ui-dialog-popup')
        $('#body-shadow').addClass('box-body-shadow');
        $(document).scrollTop($('#newsletter-portlet').offset().top);
    });*/

    if(popUp === 'true'){
        mainDiv.classList.add("popUp");
        $(window).on('resize', moveSubmitButton);
        $('input').each(function() {
            if ($(this).val() == "") {
                var allElements = document.getElementsByTagName('label');
                for (var i = 0, n = allElements.length; i < n; i++) {
                }
            }
        });
    } else {
        mainDiv.classList.remove("popUp");
    }

    $(document).ready(function(){
       $("#_de_hays_osgi_liferay_webform_newsletter_portlet_NewsLetterPortlet_INSTANCE_ptol_email").focus(function(){
            $("#legal-content").show();
       });
       if($("#_de_hays_osgi_liferay_webform_newsletter_portlet_NewsLetterPortlet_INSTANCE_ptol_email").val() !== ""){
            $("#legal-content").show();
       }
    });
</script>

<script>
    $(function(){
        $('.newsletter-portlet').dialog({
        autoOpen: false,
        modal: true,
        height: 'auto',
        width: '60%',
        transform: 'translate(50%, 50%)',
        close: function(event, ui){

            setTimeout(function(){
                $('form')[2].reset();}, 500);

            $('form')[2].reset();
            $('#message-div').html('');
            $('#topformBody').show();
            $('#bottomformBody').show();
            $('#textLegalContent').show();
            htmlBody.classList.remove('hidescrl');
            htmlBodysc.classList.remove('hidescrl');
            $(document).scrollTop($('#newsletterTeaser').offset().top);
            $('#body-shadow').removeClass('box-body-shadow');
            $('label.contact-input-label').removeClass('active-label').removeClass('contact-input-success-label-focus');
            $('input.contact-form-control').removeClass('success-field');
            $("#legal-content").hide();
        }

    })

    $('#btn-newsletterPopup').click(function(){
    $('.newsletter-portlet').dialog('open')
    })

    $('#btn-newsletterPopup-mobile').click(function(){

    $('.newsletter-portlet').dialog('open')
    })

<h2>
  <strong> Important hard and soft skills for technical writers</strong>
</h2></div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-fd0af366-c0b3-04ec-a53b-d2332c56d47a " style=""><div id="fragment-bcd14edf-face-b7e7-054d-994a202d84d0"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text"><p paraeid="{8e1b0446-9ca6-4065-b049-98cf64a47c8d}{248}" paraid="708007261">Technical writers need in-depth expertise in the <a href="https://www.hays.de/en/recruitment-services/industries" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">industries</a> in which they work, as well as knowledge of relevant technologies. They should also be confident in using IT, CMS and graphics programmes. A key skill is their excellent ability to express themselves linguistically, which enables them to present even very complex issues simply.&nbsp;</p>

<p paraeid="{0ac201dc-12a7-43c1-8ca1-9c93edecda82}{25}" paraid="241079948">Technical writers need these <strong>hard skills:</strong>&nbsp;</p>
</div></div><style>.component-paragraph img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-223ed616-2d95-b578-aec7-befd90b1f4a8 " style=""><div id="fragment-b41c4f92-33fe-04a9-f6c5-c55e44febecc"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text"><ul>
	<li aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-level="1" data-aria-posinset="1" data-font="Symbol" data-leveltext="" data-list-defn-props="{&quot;335552541&quot;:1,&quot;335559685&quot;:720,&quot;335559991&quot;:360,&quot;469769226&quot;:&quot;Symbol&quot;,&quot;469769242&quot;:[8226],&quot;469777803&quot;:&quot;left&quot;,&quot;469777804&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;469777815&quot;:&quot;multilevel&quot;}" data-listid="2" role="listitem">
	<p paraeid="{0ac201dc-12a7-43c1-8ca1-9c93edecda82}{37}" paraid="1573007476">Relevant studies or vocational training&nbsp;</p>
	</li>
	<li aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-level="1" data-aria-posinset="5" data-font="Symbol" data-leveltext="" data-list-defn-props="{&quot;335552541&quot;:1,&quot;335559685&quot;:720,&quot;335559991&quot;:360,&quot;469769226&quot;:&quot;Symbol&quot;,&quot;469769242&quot;:[8226],&quot;469777803&quot;:&quot;left&quot;,&quot;469777804&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;469777815&quot;:&quot;multilevel&quot;}" data-listid="2" role="listitem">
	<p paraeid="{0ac201dc-12a7-43c1-8ca1-9c93edecda82}{61}" paraid="2113888307">Clear spelling&nbsp;</p>
	</li>
	<li aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-level="1" data-aria-posinset="4" data-font="Symbol" data-leveltext="" data-list-defn-props="{&quot;335552541&quot;:1,&quot;335559685&quot;:720,&quot;335559991&quot;:360,&quot;469769226&quot;:&quot;Symbol&quot;,&quot;469769242&quot;:[8226],&quot;469777803&quot;:&quot;left&quot;,&quot;469777804&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;469777815&quot;:&quot;multilevel&quot;}" data-listid="2" role="listitem">
	<p paraeid="{0ac201dc-12a7-43c1-8ca1-9c93edecda82}{55}" paraid="635602031">Confident use of word processing software and other necessary tools&nbsp;</p>
	</li>
	<li aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-level="1" data-aria-posinset="3" data-font="Symbol" data-leveltext="" data-list-defn-props="{&quot;335552541&quot;:1,&quot;335559685&quot;:720,&quot;335559991&quot;:360,&quot;469769226&quot;:&quot;Symbol&quot;,&quot;469769242&quot;:[8226],&quot;469777803&quot;:&quot;left&quot;,&quot;469777804&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;469777815&quot;:&quot;multilevel&quot;}" data-listid="2" role="listitem">
	<p paraeid="{0ac201dc-12a7-43c1-8ca1-9c93edecda82}{49}" paraid="1095735906">Very good technical understanding&nbsp;</p>
	</li>
	<li aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-level="1" data-aria-posinset="2" data-font="Symbol" data-leveltext="" data-list-defn-props="{&quot;335552541&quot;:1,&quot;335559685&quot;:720,&quot;335559991&quot;:360,&quot;469769226&quot;:&quot;Symbol&quot;,&quot;469769242&quot;:[8226],&quot;469777803&quot;:&quot;left&quot;,&quot;469777804&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;469777815&quot;:&quot;multilevel&quot;}" data-listid="2" role="listitem">
	<p paraeid="{0ac201dc-12a7-43c1-8ca1-9c93edecda82}{43}" paraid="2110376396">Excellent German and English language skills&nbsp;</p>
	</li>
</ul>
</div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-fe8b06c1-0140-c518-9f91-5f21dc1305d6 " style=""><div id="fragment-43f83437-5d0e-dbad-cadd-8a92018535cb"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text">And these <strong>soft skills </strong>are required:&nbsp;</div></div></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-d20f0f5a-5bc1-73c0-8221-37ebb8a25548 " style=""><div id="fragment-607a35ad-7c26-bea6-bdd3-ce3718d6297e"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text"><ul>
	<li aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-level="1" data-aria-posinset="6" data-font="Symbol" data-leveltext="" data-list-defn-props="{&quot;335552541&quot;:1,&quot;335559685&quot;:720,&quot;335559991&quot;:360,&quot;469769226&quot;:&quot;Symbol&quot;,&quot;469769242&quot;:[8226],&quot;469777803&quot;:&quot;left&quot;,&quot;469777804&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;469777815&quot;:&quot;multilevel&quot;}" data-listid="2" role="listitem">

<h2>
  Career as a technical writer: <br /><strong> opportunities on the labour market  </strong>
</h2></div></div><style>.component-html img {
	max-width: 100%;
}</style></div><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-58473260-fdf4-8aae-3aa6-fbfe620c186f lfr-layout-structure-item-row " style=""><div class="row align-items-lg-start align-items-sm-start align-items-start align-items-md-start flex-lg-row flex-sm-row flex-row flex-md-row"><div class="col col-lg-8 col-sm-12 col-12 col-md-8"><div class="lfr-layout-structure-item-basic-component-paragraph lfr-layout-structure-item-df7c705e-afdb-7be2-e7fe-b7edfd72b0c1 " style=""><div id="fragment-00f78fa4-63e7-6631-041a-fc910d8f9c24"> <div class="clearfix component-paragraph text-break" data-lfr-editable-id="element-text" data-lfr-editable-type="rich-text"><p paraeid="{0ac201dc-12a7-43c1-8ca1-9c93edecda82}{125}" paraid="518886617">Companies that manufacture and sell technical products are also obliged to supply operating instructions. Technical writers are therefore in demand in many different areas. According to the Association for Technical Communication, around 90,000 people currently work in technical communication in Germany.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>

<div id="hh-loader-gwdc_" class="hh-item hh-item4">
    <div class="circle circle1"></div>
    <div class="circle circle2"></div>
    <div class="circle circle3"></div>

<script>
    if (window.location.protocol.indexOf('https') == 0){
        var el = document.createElement('meta')
        el.setAttribute('http-equiv', 'Content-Security-Policy')
        el.setAttribute('content', 'upgrade-insecure-requests')
        document.head.append(el)
    }
    var href = document.location.origin;
    href += "/en/jobsearch/job-offers"+ "/";
    href += 'p/1/';
    var s = "Technischer Redakteur";
    s = s.replace(/\s/g, '+');
    console.log(s);
    href += '?q='+s+'&e=false';
    href += '&saveFilter=false';
    console.log("fetching from " + href);

    function loadJobLinks() {
        console.log("imloaded");
        var langAttributeValue = $('html').attr('lang');
        var buttonTitle;

        if(langAttributeValue === 'de-CH' || langAttributeValue === 'de-DE' ){
            buttonTitle = 'Jetzt ansehen';
        } else if (langAttributeValue === 'fr-FR') {
            buttonTitle = 'Regarder maintenant';
        }
        else if (langAttributeValue === 'en-GB') {
            buttonTitle = 'View now';
        }
        else {
            buttonTitle = 'Læs mere';
        }
        if ($(".search__result").length != 0){
            setTimeout(function() {
                $('.search__result').each(function(index){
                    var watchNowLink = $(this).find('.search__result__link').attr('href');
                    if($(this).find('.search__result__meta')){
                        $(this).append('<a class="h-job-profiles__related-jobs-links" href="'+watchNowLink+'">'+buttonTitle+'</a>');
                    }
                })
            }, 1000);}
    }

    function insert_jobs(){
        $("#publish-jobs-gwdc_").load(href + ' .search__results .search__result:nth-child(-n+21)', function() {
            $('.search__result.text-center').remove();
            $('a.search__result__link').click (function(e){
                e.preventDefault();
                dataLayer.push(
                    {
                        'event': 'Link-Klick',
                        'eventkategorie': 'job-publisher-content-template',
                        'eventaktion': 'clicked' +$(this).attr("href")+ 'von:' + document.location.href,
                        'eventlabel': 'Klick auf einen Job'
                    }
                );
                console.log("datalayer is sent.");
                console.log($(this).attr("href"));
                var addressValue = $(this).attr("href");
                setTimeout(function () {
                    window.location.href = addressValue;
                }, 500);
            });

            setTimeout(function(){
                $("#publish-jobs-gwdc_").slick({
                    /* variableWidth: true,*/
                    dots: true,
                    infinite: true,
                    slidesToShow:  3,
                    slidesToScroll: 1,
                    responsive: [
                        {
                            breakpoint: 900,
                            settings: {
                                slidesToShow: 2,
                                slidesToScroll: 1
                            }
                        },
                        {
                            breakpoint: 576,
                            settings: {
                                slidesToShow: 1,
                                slidesToScroll: 1,
                                centerMode:true,
                                centerPadding:'0'
                            }
                        }
                    ]
                });
                $(".lazy").slick({
                    lazyLoad: 'ondemand', // ondemand progressive anticipated
                    infinite: true
                });
            }, 100);

            loadJobLinks();


            $("#hh-loader-gwdc_").hide();
            if ($('#publish-jobs-gwdc_').is(':empty')) {
                console.log("No result");
                var h2Tag = document.createElement('H3');
                if ($('html').attr('lang') == "de-CH" || $('html').attr('lang') == "de-DE") {
                    h2Tag.innerHTML = "Für dieses Jobprofil wurden keine vakanten Stellen gefunden.";
                }
                if ($('html').attr('lang') == "fr-FR") {
                    h2Tag.innerHTML = "Aucun poste vacant trouvé pour ce profil.";
                }
                if ($('html').attr('lang') == "en-GB") {
                    h2Tag.innerHTML = "No job opportunities found for this profile.";
                }
                $('#publish-jobs-nojob-gwdc_').prepend(h2Tag);
            }
        });
    }
    insert_jobs();
</script>

            <a class="fold-link-open  folded-content "></a>
        </div>
        <div class="fold-content  unfolded "><p>In Germany, technical writers earn an average of € 46,800 gross per year. At entry level, the average salary is €41,000 per year.</p></div>

	<div class="fold-template-mobile" onclick="dataLayer.push({'event': 'fold-content', 'eventkategorie': 'Accordion - geklickt','eventaktion': 'von:' + window.location.href,'eventlabel': 'How much does a technical writer earn?'});">
	    <div class="fold-link">
            <a class="fold-link-close  folded-content "></a>
            <a class="fold-link-open "></a>

<script>
    var handlerAttached = false;
    $(document).ready(function () {
        $( "a.fold-link-open" ).click(function() {
            $(this).parent().parent().children('.fold-content-teaser').hide();
            $(this).parent().parent().children('.fold-content').show();
            $(this).css('display', 'none');
            $(this).parent().children('a.fold-link-close').css('display', 'inline-block');
        });

	$( "a.fold-link-close" ).click(function() {
        $(this).parent().parent().children('.fold-content').hide();
        $(this).parent().parent().children('.fold-content-teaser').show();
        $(this).parent().children('a.fold-link-open').css('display', 'inline-block');
		$(this).css('display', 'none');
    });

    if (handlerAttached == false) {
        $( "div.fold-content-template div.fold-headline h3" ).click(function() {
                    var contentTemplateDiv = $(this).parentsUntil("div.fold-content-template").parent();
                    var contentDiv = contentTemplateDiv.find('.fold-content');
                    var contentTeaser = contentTemplateDiv.find('.fold-content-teaser');
                    var aFoldLinkOpen = contentTemplateDiv.find('a.fold-link-open');
                    var aFoldLinkClose = contentTemplateDiv.find('a.fold-link-close');
                    if (contentDiv.css('display') == 'none') {
                    aFoldLinkOpen.css('display', 'none');
                    aFoldLinkClose.css('display', 'inline-block');
                    contentDiv.fadeIn('fast');
                    contentTeaser.toggle();
                    } else {
                    aFoldLinkOpen.css('display', 'inline-block');
                    aFoldLinkClose.css('display', 'none');
                    contentDiv.fadeOut('fast');
                    contentTeaser.toggle();
                    }
                });
                handlerAttached = true;
                }
    });
</script>


			
		</div>

		<div class="journal-content-article " data-analytics-asset-id="3474117315" data-analytics-asset-title="fold-content-template-jobprofil-technischer-redakteur-faq-3" data-analytics-asset-type="web-content" data-analytics-web-content-resource-pk="3474117317">
			

			<div class="fold-content-template  parchmentbg-nopattern ">
    <div class="fold-headline">
            <h3 class="h-h3"><a id="">What degree do you need to become a technical writer?</a></h3>
    </div>
    <div class="fold-template-desktop" onclick="dataLayer.push({'event': 'fold-content', 'eventkategorie': 'Accordion - geklickt','eventaktion': 'von:' + window.location.href,'eventlabel': 'What degree do you need to become a technical writer?'});">
	    <div class="fold-link">
            <a class="fold-link-close  folded-content "></a>
            <a class="fold-link-open "></a>

<script>
    var handlerAttached = false;
    $(document).ready(function () {
        $( "a.fold-link-open" ).click(function() {
            $(this).parent().parent().children('.fold-content-teaser').hide();
            $(this).parent().parent().children('.fold-content').show();
            $(this).css('display', 'none');
            $(this).parent().children('a.fold-link-close').css('display', 'inline-block');
        });

	$( "a.fold-link-close" ).click(function() {
        $(this).parent().parent().children('.fold-content').hide();
        $(this).parent().parent().children('.fold-content-teaser').show();
        $(this).parent().children('a.fold-link-open').css('display', 'inline-block');
		$(this).css('display', 'none');
    });

    if (handlerAttached == false) {
        $( "div.fold-content-template div.fold-headline h3" ).click(function() {
                    var contentTemplateDiv = $(this).parentsUntil("div.fold-content-template").parent();
                    var contentDiv = contentTemplateDiv.find('.fold-content');
                    var contentTeaser = contentTemplateDiv.find('.fold-content-teaser');
                    var aFoldLinkOpen = contentTemplateDiv.find('a.fold-link-open');
                    var aFoldLinkClose = contentTemplateDiv.find('a.fold-link-close');
                    if (contentDiv.css('display') == 'none') {
                    aFoldLinkOpen.css('display', 'none');
                    aFoldLinkClose.css('display', 'inline-block');
                    contentDiv.fadeIn('fast');
                    contentTeaser.toggle();
                    } else {
                    aFoldLinkOpen.css('display', 'inline-block');
                    aFoldLinkClose.css('display', 'none');
                    contentDiv.fadeOut('fast');
                    contentTeaser.toggle();
                    }
                });
                handlerAttached = true;
                }
    });
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

	
		Liferay.Portlet.register('com_liferay_asset_publisher_web_portlet_AssetPublisherPortlet_INSTANCE_msto');
	

	Liferay.Portlet.onLoad(
		{
			canEditTitle: false,
			columnPos: 0,
			isStatic: 'end',
			namespacedId: 'p_p_id_com_liferay_asset_publisher_web_portlet_AssetPublisherPortlet_INSTANCE_msto_',
			portletId: 'com_liferay_asset_publisher_web_portlet_AssetPublisherPortlet_INSTANCE_msto',
			refreshURL: '\x2fen\x2fc\x2fportal\x2frender_portlet\x3fp_l_id\x3d3400417517\x26p_p_id\x3dcom_liferay_asset_publisher_web_portlet_AssetPublisherPortlet_INSTANCE_msto\x26p_p_lifecycle\x3d0\x26p_t_lifecycle\x3d0\x26p_p_state\x3dnormal\x26p_p_mode\x3dview\x26p_p_col_id\x3dnull\x26p_p_col_pos\x3dnull\x26p_p_col_count\x3dnull\x26p_p_static\x3d1\x26p_p_isolated\x3d1\x26currentURL\x3d\x252Fen\x252Fjob-profiles\x252Ftechnical-writer',
			refreshURLData: {}
		}
	);

(function() {var $ = AUI.$;var _ = AUI._;
	var onDestroyPortlet = function () {
		Liferay.detach('messagePosted', onMessagePosted);
		Liferay.detach('destroyPortlet', onDestroyPortlet);
	};

	Liferay.on('destroyPortlet', onDestroyPortlet);

	var onMessagePosted = function (event) {
		if (window.Analytics) {
			const eventProperties = {
				className: event.className,
				classPK: event.classPK,
				commentId: event.commentId,
				text: event.text,
			};

			const blogNode = document.querySelector(
				'[data-analytics-asset-id="' + event.classPK + '"]'
			);

			const dmNode = document.querySelector(
				'[data-analytics-file-entry-id="' + event.classPK + '"]'
			);

			if (blogNode) {
				eventProperties.title = blogNode.dataset.analyticsAssetTitle;
			}
			else if (dmNode) {
				eventProperties.title = dmNode.dataset.analyticsFileEntryTitle;
			}

			Analytics.send('posted', 'Comment', eventProperties);
		}
	};

	Liferay.on('messagePosted', onMessagePosted);
})();

	function getValueByAttribute(node, attr) {
		return (
			node.dataset[attr] ||
			(node.parentElement && node.parentElement.dataset[attr])
		);
	}

	function sendDocumentDownloadedAnalyticsEvent(anchor) {
		var fileEntryId = getValueByAttribute(
			anchor,
			'analyticsFileEntryId'
		);
		var title = getValueByAttribute(
			anchor,
			'analyticsFileEntryTitle'
		);
		var version = getValueByAttribute(
			anchor,
			'analyticsFileEntryVersion'
		);

		if (fileEntryId) {
			Analytics.send('documentDownloaded', 'Document', {
				groupId: themeDisplay.getScopeGroupId(),
				fileEntryId,
				preview: !!window._com_liferay_document_library_analytics_isViewFileEntry,
				title,
				version,
			});
		}
	}

	function handleDownloadClick(event) {
		if (window.Analytics) {
			if (event.target.nodeName.toLowerCase() === 'a') {
				sendDocumentDownloadedAnalyticsEvent(
					event.target
				);
			}
			else if (
				event.target.parentNode &&
				event.target.parentNode.nodeName.toLowerCase() === 'a'
			) {
				sendDocumentDownloadedAnalyticsEvent(
					event.target.parentNode
				);
			}
			else {
				var target = event.target;
				var matchTextContent =
					target.textContent &&
					target.textContent.toLowerCase() ===
						'download';
				var matchTitle =
					target.title && target.title.toLowerCase() === 'download';
				var matchAction = target.action === 'download';
				var matchLexiconIcon = !!target.querySelector(
					'.lexicon-icon-download'
				);
				var matchLexiconClassName = target.classList.contains(
					'lexicon-icon-download'
				);
				var matchParentTitle =
					target.parentNode &&
					target.parentNode.title &&
					target.parentNode.title.toLowerCase() === 'download';
				var matchParentLexiconClassName =
					target.parentNode &&
					target.parentNode.classList.contains('lexicon-icon-download');

				if (
					matchTextContent ||
					matchTitle ||
					matchParentTitle ||
					matchAction ||
					matchLexiconIcon ||
					matchLexiconClassName ||
					matchParentLexiconClassName
				) {
					var selectedFiles = document.querySelectorAll(
						'.form .custom-control-input:checked'
					);

					selectedFiles.forEach(({value}) => {
						var selectedFile = document.querySelector(
							'[data-analytics-file-entry-id="' + value + '"]'
						);

						sendDocumentDownloadedAnalyticsEvent(
							selectedFile
						);
					});
				}
			}
		}
	}

	Liferay.once('destroyPortlet', () => {
		document.body.removeEventListener(
			'click',
			handleDownloadClick
		);
	});

	Liferay.once('portletReady', () => {
		document.body.addEventListener(
			'click',
			handleDownloadClick
		);
	});

(function() {var $ = AUI.$;var _ = AUI._;
	var onVote = function (event) {
		if (window.Analytics) {
			let title = event.contentTitle;

			if (!title) {
				const dmNode = document.querySelector(
					'[data-analytics-file-entry-id="' + event.classPK + '"]'
				);

				if (dmNode) {
					title = dmNode.dataset.analyticsFileEntryTitle;
				}
			}

			Analytics.send('VOTE', 'Ratings', {
				className: event.className,
				classPK: event.classPK,
				ratingType: event.ratingType,
				score: event.score,
				title,
			});
		}
	};

	var onDestroyPortlet = function () {
		Liferay.detach('ratings:vote', onVote);
		Liferay.detach('destroyPortlet', onDestroyPortlet);
	};

	Liferay.on('ratings:vote', onVote);
	Liferay.on('destroyPortlet', onDestroyPortlet);
})();
(function() {var $ = AUI.$;var _ = AUI._;
	var onShare = function (data) {
		if (window.Analytics) {
			Analytics.send('shared', 'SocialBookmarks', {
				className: data.className,
				classPK: data.classPK,
				type: data.type,
				url: data.url,
			});
		}
	};

	var onDestroyPortlet = function () {
		Liferay.detach('socialBookmarks:share', onShare);
		Liferay.detach('destroyPortlet', onDestroyPortlet);
	};

	Liferay.on('socialBookmarks:share', onShare);
	Liferay.on('destroyPortlet', onDestroyPortlet);
})();

	if (window.svg4everybody && Liferay.Data.ICONS_INLINE_SVG) {
		svg4everybody(
			{
				polyfill: true,
				validate: function (src, svg, use) {
					return !src || !src.startsWith('#');
				}
			}
		);
	}

(function() {var $ = AUI.$;var _ = AUI._;
	Liferay.Util.delegate(
		document,
		'focusin',
		'.portlet',
		function(event) {
			event.delegateTarget.closest('.portlet').classList.add('open');
		}
	);

	Liferay.Util.delegate(
		document,
		'focusout',
		'.portlet',
		function(event) {
			event.delegateTarget.closest('.portlet').classList.remove('open');
		}
	);
})();

				function loadMoinScript(url, id, callback) {
  var script = document.createElement("script");
  script.type = "text/javascript";
  if (script.readyState) {
    script.onreadystatechange = function () {
      if (script.readyState == "loaded" || script.readyState == "complete") {
        script.onreadystatechange = null;
        callback();
      }
    };
  } else {
    script.readyState = function () {
      callback();
    };
  }
  script.src = url;
  if (id) {
    script.id = id;
  }
  document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
}
window.addEventListener("load", function () {
  if (typeof truste !== "undefined") {
    const TRUST_FUNCTIONAL = 2;
    let result = truste.cma.callApi("getConsentDecision", window.location.host);
    if (
      result.consentDecision >= TRUST_FUNCTIONAL &&
      !window.location.href.includes("/lp/")
    ) {
      if (document.documentElement.lang == "de-DE") {
        loadMoinScript(
          "https://widget.moin.ai/moin-loader.js?id=ee05741e33c129f2532ec938462da9a13e2a95e725ffb8049cbf789431fc028c&channelid=ee05741e33c129f2532ec938462da9a13e2a95e725ffb8049cbf789431fc028c&v=" +
          Date.now(),
          "moinloader"
        );
      } else if (document.documentElement.lang == "en-GB") {
        loadMoinScript(
          "https://widget.moin.ai/moin-loader.js?id=ee05741e33c129f2532ec938462da9a13e2a95e725ffb8049cbf789431fc028c&channelid=ee05741e33c129f2532ec938462da9a13e2a95e725ffb8049cbf789431fc028c-en&v=" +
          Date.now(),
          "moinloader"
        );
      }

      loadMoinScript(
        "https://widget.moin.ai/zendesk-web-sdk.js?v=" + Date.now(),
        ""
      );
    }
  }
});



window.chatWidgetReady = function () {
  window.knowhere.api.setWidgetzIndex(50);
  window.knowhere.api.setWidgetPosition(0, 70, "px", true);
  $("#moin-ai-widget").css({ maxHeight: "95vh" });
  //  window.knowhere.api.hideWidget();
  let moin_message = null;
  const isMobile = /iPhone|iPad|iPod|Android/i.test(navigator.userAgent);

  window.knowhere.api.on('widget.interaction', function (data) {
    moin_message = data;
    console.log('WIDGET HANDLER', JSON.stringify(moin_message));

    //console.log(' WIDGET HANDLER', JSON.stringify(data.message.action),JSON.stringify(data.message.source));
    dataLayer.push({ 'event': 'moin-ai-chat', 'eventkategorie': 'moin_ai', 'eventaktion': 'widget-interaction', 'eventlabel': "current.page: " + window.location.href + " is.mobile " + isMobile + " data.message.action:" + JSON.stringify(data.message.action) + ", data.message.message:" + JSON.stringify(data.message.source) });
  })

  window.knowhere.api.on('user.click', function (data) {
    moin_message = data;
   // console.log('CLICK HANDLER', JSON.stringify(moin_message));

    //console.log(' CLICK HANDLER', JSON.stringify(data.message.source),JSON.stringify(data.message.text),JSON.stringify(data.message.target));
    dataLayer.push({ 'event': 'moin-ai-chat', 'eventkategorie': 'moin_ai', 'eventaktion': 'user-click', 'eventlabel': "current.page: " + window.location.href + " is.mobile " + isMobile + " data.message.source:" + JSON.stringify(data.message.source) + ", data.message.text:" + JSON.stringify(data.message.text) + ", data.message.target:" + JSON.stringify(data.message.target) });
  })

  window.knowhere.api.on('user.input', function (data) {
    moin_message = data;
    //console.log('USER HANDLER', JSON.stringify(moin_message));

    //console.log(' USER HANDLER', JSON.stringify(data.message.action),JSON.stringify(data.message.message));
    dataLayer.push({ 'event': 'moin-ai-chat', 'eventkategorie': 'moin_ai', 'eventaktion': 'user-input', 'eventlabel': "current.page: " + window.location.href + " is.mobile " + isMobile + " data.message.action:" + JSON.stringify(data.message.action)});
  })
};

  $(this).attr(
    "onclick",
    "dataLayer.push({'event': 'Think Ahead','eventkategorie': 'Navigationspunkt','eventaktion': 'menu-name: '+ this.innerText,'eventlabel':$(this).attr('href')});"
  );
});

//Haysworld buttons track

$(".h-btn-track-extern").each(function () {
  $(this).attr(
    "onclick",
    "dataLayer.push({'event': 'Button', 'eventkategorie': 'externer Link', 'eventaktion': window.location.href, 'eventlabel': $(this).attr('href')});"
  );
});

$("a").each(function () {
  if ($(this).attr("href") && !$(this).attr("onclick")) {
    var hrefValue = $(this).attr('href');
    var eventKategorie = hrefValue.includes(".hays.") || hrefValue.startsWith("/") ? "interner Link" : "externer Link";
    var currentLocation = window.location.pathname;
    var eventType = $(this).hasClass("hays-btn") || $(this).hasClass("h-btn") ? "Button" : "Link-Klick";
    var eventLabel = hrefValue;

    // Remove "https://www." or "https://" if it's an external link
    if (eventKategorie === "externer Link") {
      if (eventLabel.startsWith("https://www.")) {
        eventLabel = eventLabel.replace("https://www.", "");
      } else if (eventLabel.startsWith("https://")) {
        eventLabel = eventLabel.replace("https://", "");
      }
    }

    $(this).attr(
      "onclick",
      "dataLayer.push({'event': '" + eventType + "', 'eventkategorie': '" + eventKategorie + "', 'eventaktion': 'von: " + currentLocation + "', 'eventlabel': 'nach: " + eventLabel + "'});"
    );
  }
});

    $(document).ready(function(){
        var layoutStory = $.trim('3563 778 ');

        $(".top-navigation-flyout-link").find(".layout_"+layoutWithoutChild).css("color", "#002776");

            $(".popup__menu").addClass("hidden");
            $(".button_back_to_mobile_level").removeClass("hidden");
            $(".row.border_bottom_mobile_menu").addClass("hidden");
            $(".mobile-navitem-title").addClass("hidden");
            $(".row.button_back_to_mobile_menu").removeClass("hidden");
            $(".mobile-navitem-title.collapse_my_hays_mobile_menu").removeClass("hidden");
            $(".popup__menu.collapse_my_hays_mobile_menu").removeClass("hidden");
        } else if (mobileLayoutStory != "" && $(".mobile_layout_"+mobileLayoutStory).length > 1) {
            $(".row.border_bottom_mobile_menu").addClass("hidden");
            $(".row.button_back_to_mobile_menu").removeClass("hidden");
            $("span.button_back_to_mobile_menu").removeClass("hidden");
            $(".button_back_to_mobile_level").removeClass("hidden");

            $(".mobile-navitem-title").addClass("hidden");
            $(".mobile_layout_"+mobileLayoutStory).removeClass("hidden");
        }

        $("#navigation-container").children().each(function(item) {
            if ($(this).find(".top-navigation-flyout").length != 0) {
                $(this).mouseenter(function() {
                    $("#body-shadow").addClass("body-shadow-show");
                }).mouseleave(function() {
                    $("#body-shadow").removeClass("body-shadow-show");
                    navigationHistory(layoutStory);
                });
            }
       });

        $(".nav-list__item").mouseenter(function() {
            let count = $(this).children().find("ul:lt(1)").children().length;
            if ($(this).children(".container-grid:lt(1)").hasClass("container-grid-third") || $(this).parent().children().length > count && count != 0 && !$(this).find(".nav-list:lt(1)").hasClass("scrollbar-nav-items")) {
                $(this).children(".container-grid:lt(1)").addClass("compare-children-height");
                $(this).find(".nav-list:lt(1)").addClass("compare-children-height-ul");
            }
        }).mouseleave(function() {
            $(this).children(".container-grid:lt(1)").removeClass("compare-children-height");
            $(this).find(".nav-list:lt(1)").removeClass("compare-children-height-ul");
        });

        });

        $(".container-grid").hover(function() {
            $(this).parents(".top-navigation-flyout-link").find(".static-flyout-link").toggleClass("link-active");
            toggleSelectedLayoutStory(layoutStory, "removeClass");
        });

                <script>
                    setCookie("hays_rdrt", window.location.pathname + window.location.search);
                    const utmString = getUtmPartOfString(window.location.pathname + window.location.search);


                    function setCookie(name, value) {
                        const date = new Date();
                        date.setTime(date.getTime() + (1*24*60*60*1000));
                        let expires = "expires="+ date.toUTCString();
                        document.cookie = name + "=" + value + ";" + expires + ";path=/";
                    }

                    function setUTMCookie(name, value) {
                        const date = new Date();
                        date.setTime(date.getTime() + (15*60*1000));
                        let expires = "expires="+ date.toUTCString();
                        document.cookie = name + "=" + value + ";" + expires + ";path=/";
                    }

                    function getCookie(name){
                        const cookies = document.cookie.split(';');
                        for (let i = 0; i < cookies.length; i++){
                            const cookie = cookies[i].trim();
                            if(cookie.startsWith(name + '=')){
                                return cookie.substring(name.length + 1);
                            }
                        }
                        return null;
                    }

                    function getUtmPartOfString(url){
                        const utmParams = extractAndCheckUtm(url);
                        const utmParamsUrl = window.location.pathname;
                        if(utmParams){
                            let modiefiedUtm = utmParams.replace(/=/g, "/");
                            setUTMCookie('utm_params',encodeURIComponent(modiefiedUtm));
                            setUTMCookie('utm_params_initial',utmParamsUrl);
                            return modiefiedUtm;
                        }else {
                            const storedQuery = getCookie('utm_params');
                            if(storedQuery && storedQuery.includes("utm")){
                                return storedQuery;
                            }
                        }
                        return null;
                    }

                    function extractAndCheckUtm(url){
                        const utmStringIndex = url.indexOf("?");
                        if(utmStringIndex !== -1){
                            const extractUtm = url.substring(utmStringIndex + 1)
                            return extractUtm.includes("utm") ? extractUtm : null;
                        }
                        return null;
                    }
                </script>

                <script>
                    var input = document.getElementById("what");
                    input.addEventListener("keypress", function(event) {
                        if (event.key === "Enter") {
                            event.preventDefault();
                            document.getElementById("searchbar-trigger-btn").click();
                        }
                    });
                </script>
